### <a id="inductive-types-h-s-p-and-v">Inductive Types H, S, P, and V</a>

This section presents the [UALib.Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="341" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="345" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="353" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="365" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="379" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="386" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

<a id="391" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="396" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="403" href="UALib.Algebras.html" class="Module">UALib.Algebras</a> <a id="418" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="424" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="425" href="UALib.Algebras.Signatures.html#1377" class="Function">Signature</a><a id="434" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="436" href="universes.html#613" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a><a id="437" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="439" href="universes.html#617" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="440" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="442" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a><a id="449" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="451" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#3472" class="Function Operator">_↠_</a><a id="454" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="456" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="461" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="468" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html" class="Module">UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries</a> <a id="496" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="502" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="503" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="517" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="519" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="527" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="529" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">_̇</a><a id="531" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="534" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="541" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html" class="Module">UALib.Varieties.Varieties</a> <a id="567" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="568" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a> <a id="570" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="572" href="UALib.Algebras.Signatures.html#1377" class="Function">Signature</a> <a id="582" href="universes.html#613" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a> <a id="584" href="universes.html#617" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="585" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="587" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#587" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="591" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="593" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="607" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="609" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="616" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="621" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="628" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html" class="Module">UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic</a><a id="659" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="660" class="Argument">𝑆</a> <a id="662" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="664" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="665" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="667" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#587" class="Bound">gfe</a><a id="670" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="672" class="Keyword">public</a>

</pre>


Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.




#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphic closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2280" class="Comment">--Closure wrt H</a>

#### <a id="subalgebraic-closure">Subalgebraic closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of a class of algebras that is closed under the taking of subalgebras is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2939" class="Comment">--Closure wrt S</a>
<a id="2955" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="2960" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2960" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="2962" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2963" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2963" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2965" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2965" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="2967" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2969" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="2977" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="2979" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2979" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="2981" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2983" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="2988" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2989" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="2997" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2963" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2999" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3000" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3002" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3003" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="3006" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2963" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3007" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3010" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="S.ssub"></a><a id="3180" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3180" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a>  <a id="3186" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3188" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3189" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3189" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3191" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3193" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3201" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3239" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3241" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3206" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3243" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3528"   <a id="S.ssubw"></a><a id="3259" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3259" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="3265" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3267" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3268" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3268" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3270" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3270" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3272" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3274" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3282" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="3284" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3285" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3287" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3289" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3268" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3291" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3293" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2960" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="3294" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3295" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2963" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3296" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3298" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2965" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3299" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3301" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2979" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3303" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3305" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3270" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3307" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3528" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="3309" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3268" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3311" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3313" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3270" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3315" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3317" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2960" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3319" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2979" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="S.siso"></a><a id="3323" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3323" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a>  <a id="3329" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3331" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3332" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2979" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of an class of algebras closed under the taking of arbitrary products is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3655" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3660" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3660" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3662" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3663" <a id="3683" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3688" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3689" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3660" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4174" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4175" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3663" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4176" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4178" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3663" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4179" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4181" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3679" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4183" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4185" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4133" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4187" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1114" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4189" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4150" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4191" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4193" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4150" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4195" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4197" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3660" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4199" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3679" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4203" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4203" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4210" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4212" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4213" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4213" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4215" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4215" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4217" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4219" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4227" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4229" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4230" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4232" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4234" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4213" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4236" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4238" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3660" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4239" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4240" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3663" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4241" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4243" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3665" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4244" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4246" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3679" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4248" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4250" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4213" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4252" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1114" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4254" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4215" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4256" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4258" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4215" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4260" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4262" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3660" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4264" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3679" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="varietal-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will denote it by `V`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4604" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="4609" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4609" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4611" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4612" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4614" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4614" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4616" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4618" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="4626" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="4628" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4628" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4630" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4632" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4637" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4638" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4646" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4648" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4649" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4651" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="4654" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4655" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4658" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="4661" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4666" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4667" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4675" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4676" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4678" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4680" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4614" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4681" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4683" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4684" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4686" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a><a id="4688" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4689" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4691" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4693" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4614" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4694" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4697" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="V.vbase"></a><a id="4705" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4705" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a>  <a id="4712" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4714" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4715" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4715" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4717" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4719" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4727" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4729" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4730" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4732" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4734" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4715" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4736" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4738" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4628" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4740" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4742" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#4395" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="4751" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4715" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4753" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4614" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4755" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4757" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4609" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4759" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4628" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="5230" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5217" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="5232" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5234" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5242" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5244" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5245" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5247" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5249" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="5252" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5252" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="5254" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5256" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5257" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5226" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5259" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5252" class="Bound">i</a><a id="5260" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5262" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5264" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4609" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5265" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5266" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5267" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5269" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4614" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5270" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5272" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4628" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="5273" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5275" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5277" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="5279" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5226" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5281" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5283" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4609" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5285" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4628" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="V.visou"></a><a id="5289" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5289" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a>  <a id="5296" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5298" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5299" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5299" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5301" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5303" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5311" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5313" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5314" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5316" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5316" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5318" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5320" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5328" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5330" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5331" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5333" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5335" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5299" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5337" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5339" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4609" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5340" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5341" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5342" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5344" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5345" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5347" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4628" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5349" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5351" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5299" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5353" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1114" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5355" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5316" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5357" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5359" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5316" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5361" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5363" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4609" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5365" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4628" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="V.visow"></a><a id="5369" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5369" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a>  <a id="5376" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5378" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5379" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5379" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5381" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5381" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5383" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5385" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5393" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5395" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5396" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5398" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5400" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5379" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5402" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5404" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4609" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5405" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5406" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4612" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5407" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5409" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4614" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5410" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5412" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4628" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5414" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5416" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5379" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5418" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1114" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5420" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5381" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5422" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5424" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5381" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5426" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5428" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4609" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5430" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4628" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we represent formally what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="5782" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5782" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5793" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5795" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5796" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5796" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5798" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5800" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="5808" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5810" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5810" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5812" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5814" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5819" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5820" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5828" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5796" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5830" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5831" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5833" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5836" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5796" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5837" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5840" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5842" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5845" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5796" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5847" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5849" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5782" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="5859" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5860" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5860" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5861" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5863" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5863" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5865" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5867" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4609" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5868" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5869" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5860" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5870" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5872" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5860" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5873" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5875" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5863" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5877" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3021" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="5879" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5863" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="5882" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5882" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5890" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5892" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5893" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5893" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5895" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5897" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="5905" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5907" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5909" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5910" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5913" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5893" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5914" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="5915" href="universes.html#527" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="5917" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5919" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5882" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5927" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5927" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5929" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5931" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="5933" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5933" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5935" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="5937" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5938" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5943" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5944" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5952" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5927" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5954" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5955" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5957" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5960" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5927" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5961" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5964" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="5966" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5782" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5977" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5933" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

</pre>




#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

First, `P` is a closure operator.  This is proved by checking that `P` is *monotone*, *expansive*, and *idempotent*. The meaning of these terms will be clear from the definitions of the types that follow.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="P-mono"></a><a id="6410" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6410" class="Function">P-mono</a> <a id="6417" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6419" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6420" </pre>

Similarly, S is a closure operator.  The facts that S is idempotent and expansive won't be needed below, so we omit these, but we will make use of monotonicity of S.  Here is the proof of the latter.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="S-mono"></a><a id="7762" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7769" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7771" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7772" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7772" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="7774" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7774" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="7776" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7778" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="7786" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7788" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7788" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="7790" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7790" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="7793" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7795" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="7800" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7801" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="7809" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7772" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="7811" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="7812" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="7814" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="7817" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7772" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7818" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="7821" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7823" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7788" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="7825" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3021" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="7827" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7790" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="7830" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7832" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2960" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="7833" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7834" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7772" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7835" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7837" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7774" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="7838" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7840" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7788" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="7842" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3021" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="7844" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a>

<a id="7856" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7863" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7863" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7867" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7868" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3058" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="7874" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7874" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7875" class="Symbol">)</a>            <a id="7888" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7890" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3058" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="7896" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7897" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7863" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7901" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7874" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7902" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="7904" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7911" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7911" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7915" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7916" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3115" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="7921" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7922" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7922" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7923" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7925" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7925" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7926" class="Symbol">)</a>         <a id="7936" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7938" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3115" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="7944" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7945" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7952" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7911" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7956" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7925" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7957" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="7959" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7966" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7966" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7970" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7971" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3180" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="7975" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7976" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7976" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7977" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7979" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7979" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7980" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7982" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7982" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="7985" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7985" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="7988" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="7991" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7993" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3180" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="7998" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7999" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="8006" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7966" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="8010" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7982" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="8012" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8014" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7985" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="8018" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="8025" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8025" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="8029" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8030" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3259" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="8035" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8036" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8036" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="8037" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8039" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8039" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="8040" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8042" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8042" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="8045" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8045" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="8048" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8050" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8052" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3259" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="8058" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8059" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="8066" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8025" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="8070" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8042" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="8072" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8074" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8045" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="8078" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="8085" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8085" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="8089" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8090" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3323" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="8095" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8095" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8097" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8097" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="8099" class="Symbol">)</a>          <a id="8110" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8112" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3323" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="8117" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8118" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="8125" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8085" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="8129" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8095" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8130" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8132" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8097" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="subalgebra→S"></a><a id="8344" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8344" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="8357" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8359" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8360" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8360" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8362" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8362" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8364" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8366" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="8374" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8376" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8376" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8378" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8380" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="8385" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8386" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8394" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8360" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8396" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8397" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8399" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8402" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8360" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8403" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="8406" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8406" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8408" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8410" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8418" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8419" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8360" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8421" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="8423" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8362" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="8424" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8426" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8427" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="8430" class="Symbol">→</a>             <a id="8444" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8406" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8446" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3721" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="8466" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8376" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="9960" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11744" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="9964" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="9966" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10013" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="9969" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="9971" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="9973" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5665" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9975" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9976" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4087" class="Function">TRANS-≅</a> <a id="9984" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9985" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2929" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="9991" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9936" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="9994" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9996" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10114" class="Function">A≅SA</a><a id="10000" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="10004" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="10013" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10013" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10016" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10018" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9930" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10020" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3721" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10040" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8791" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
   <a id="10045" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10013" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10048" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10050" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8829" class="Function">S→subalgebra</a> <a id="10063" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9933" class="Bound">sA</a>
   <a id="10069" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10069" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10072" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10074" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#1432" class="Function">Subalgebra</a> <a id="10085" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10087" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10013" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10090" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="10095" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10069" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10098" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10100" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11663" class="Function">fst</a> <a id="10104" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10106" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10013" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10109" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a>
   <a id="10114" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10114" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10119" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10121" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9930" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10123" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1114" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="10125" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10127" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10069" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10130" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="10135" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10114" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10140" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10142" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11744" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10146" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10148" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11744" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10152" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10013" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10155" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="lift-alg-subP"></a><a id="10439" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10439" class="Function">lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="10453" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10455" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10456" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10456" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10458" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10458" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="10460" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10462" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="10470" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10472" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10472" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10474" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10476" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10481" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10482" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10490" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10456" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10492" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10493" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10495" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10498" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10456" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10499" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="10502" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10502" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10504" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10506" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10514" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10456" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10516" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10517" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="10520" class="Symbol">→</a>              <a id="10535" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10502" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10537" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3721" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10557" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10558" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3660" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="10559" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10560" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10456" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10561" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10563" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10456" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10564" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10566" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10472" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="10567" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="10699" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10439" class="Function">lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="10713" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10714" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10714" The next lemma would be too obvoius to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

  <a id="12352" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12352" class="Function">lAsp</a> <a id="12357" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12359" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12202" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12362" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="12364" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2960" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="12365" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12366" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3660" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="12368" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12140" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="12369" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12373" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12352" class="Function">lAsp</a> <a id="12378" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12380" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8344" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a><a id="12392" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12393" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12134" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="12395" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="12397" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12137" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="12398" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12400" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12134" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="12402" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="12404" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12137" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="12405" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12407" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3660" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="12408" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12409" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12134" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="12410" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12412" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12137" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="12413" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12415" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12140" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="12416" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12418" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12202" class="Function">lA</a><a id="12420" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12422" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12248" class="Function">lAsc</a>

  <a id="12430" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12430" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12435" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12437" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12202" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12440" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1114" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="12442" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12143" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
  <a id="12446" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12430" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12451" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12453" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4278" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="12461" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12202" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12464" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12143" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="12466" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12467" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2929" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="12473" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4843" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="12483" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12485" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12157" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

<pre class="Agda">

  <a id="13346" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13346" class="Function">β</a> <a id="13348" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13350" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Basic.html#2175" class="Function">is-homomorphism</a> <a id="13366" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13367" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13369" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13044" class="Function">SA</a><a id="13371" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13373" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13374" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13376" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12999" class="Function">𝒜</a><a id="13377" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13379" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13295" class="Function">α</a>
  <a id="13383" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13346" class="Function">β</a> <a id="13385" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13387" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="13389" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13389" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="13391" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13391" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="13393" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13395" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#587" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="13399" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="13401" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13401" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13403" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13405" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13406" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11744" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="13410" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="13412" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13159" class="Function">SA≤𝒜</a> <a id="13417" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13401" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13419" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="13420" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13422" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13389" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="13424" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13427" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13427" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13429" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13431" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13391" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="13433" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13427" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13435" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13401" class="Bound">i</a><a id="13436" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="13440" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13440" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="13442" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13444" href="MGS-Embeddings.html#384" class="Function">is-embedding</a> <a id="13457" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13295" class="Function">α</a>
  <a id="13461" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13440" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="13463" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13465" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#10144" class="Function">embedding-lift</a> <a id="13480" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12930" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="13484" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12930" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="13488" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13489" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12935" class="Bound">I</a><a id="13490" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="13492" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13044" class="Function">SA</a><a id="13494" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="13496" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12999" class="Function">𝒜</a><a id="13497" class="Symbol">}</a><a id="13498" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13236" class="Function">h</a><a id="13499" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13502" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13502" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13504" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13506" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="13508" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13159" class="Function">SA≤𝒜</a> <a id="13513" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13502" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13515" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a><a id="13516" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="13521" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13521" class="Function">⨅SA≤⨅𝒜</a> <a id="13528" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13530" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13532" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13044" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="13535" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3528" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="13537" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13539" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12999" class="Function">𝒜</a>
  <a id="13543" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13521" class="Function">⨅SA≤⨅𝒜</a> <a id="13550" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13552" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13553" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13295" class="Function">α</a> <a id="13555" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5665" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13557" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13346" class="Function">β</a><a id="13558" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13560" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5665" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13562" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13440" class="Function">γ</a>

  <a id="13567" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13567" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="13569" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13571" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13573" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12999" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="13575" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="13577" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3660" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="13579" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12927" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="13583" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13567" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="13585" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13587" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3957" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="13593" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13596" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13596" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13598" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13600" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6855" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="13607" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13608" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="13610" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11744" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="13614" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="13616" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12941" class="Bound">B≤K</a> <a id="13620" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13596" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13622" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="13624" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="13625" class="Symbol">))</a>


</pre>



#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="13841" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="13848" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13848" class="Module">_</a> <a id="13850" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13851" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13851" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="13853" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13855" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="13863" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="13865" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13865" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="13867" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13869" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="13874" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13875" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="13883" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13851" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="13885" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="13886" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="13888" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="13891" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13851" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="13892" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13895" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13896" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13896" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="13900" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13902" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="13910" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13911" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="13914" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13851" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="13915" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="13917" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="13920" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13851" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="13921" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13924" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="13932" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13932" class="Function">ov𝓾</a> <a id="13936" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13938" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a>

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this module with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="P⊆V"></a><a id="15382" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15382" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="15386" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15388" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15389" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15409" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="15414" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15415" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="15428" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15431" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15389" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15432"  <a id="15779" class="Symbol">→</a>     <a id="15785" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2960" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="15786" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15787" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15732" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15789" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15791" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15734" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="15792" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15794" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15732" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15796" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15798" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15734" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="15799" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15801" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15802" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3660" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="15803" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15804" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15732" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15805" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15807" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15734" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="15808" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15810" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15748" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="15811" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15813" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3021" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="15815" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4609" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="15816" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15817" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15732" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15818" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15820" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15734" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="15821" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15823" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15748" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="15826" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15724" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="15831" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15832" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3058" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="15837" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15838" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15838" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="15839" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15841" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15841" class="Bound">PCloA</a><a id="15846" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15848" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15850" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15382" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="15854" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15855" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4203" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="15861" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15841" class="Bound">PCloA</a> <a id="15867" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4843" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="15877" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="15879" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15724" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="15884" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15885" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3115" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="15890" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15891" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15891" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="15892" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15894" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15894" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15895" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15897" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15899" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4829" class="InductiveConstructor">vliftw</a> <a id="15906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15907" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15724" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="15912" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15894" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15913" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove the result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Algebras.Products][], the (informal) product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as `⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="class-prod-s-∈-ps"></a><a id="16552" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16552" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="16570" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16572" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16573" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16573" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16575" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16577" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="16585" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16587" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16587" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="16589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16591" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16573" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16593" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="16594" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16596" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16596" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="16598" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16600" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1078" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="16605" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16606" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="16614" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16573" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16616" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#568" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="16617" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="16619" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16622" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16573" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16623" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="16627" class="Symbol">→</a>                  <a id="16646" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#4048" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="16660" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16661" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16573" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16662" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16664" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16573" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16665" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16667" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16587" class="Bound">X</a><a id="16668" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16670" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16671" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2960" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="16673" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16596" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16674" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16676" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2739" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="16678" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16679" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3660" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="16680" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16681" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16684" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16573" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16685" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16687" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16690" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16573" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16691" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16693" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16694" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2960" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="16696" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16596" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16697" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="16701" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16552" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="16719" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16720" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16720" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16721" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16723" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16723" class="Bound">X</a><a id="16724" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16726" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16726" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16727" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="16730" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16732" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4123" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="16738" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17006" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="16745" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16746" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6702" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="16749" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#587" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="16753" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17057" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="16758" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="16761" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="17172" class="Comment">-- So, since PS⊆SP, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>
